# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
multiply matrix by itself, has to be a square matrix ^2Y5rtBBT

a network diagram present the inputs and outputs with, "weights" on the node,
to represent it as matrix the column will be the inputs and the rows the weight of
each input ^73sJlnuU

networks can be combined ^MocPegXx

consider (a, b) as the input for A and (c, d) as the output for B.
(a, b)A therefore gives the input to B and B(output of A) gives the output of B ^pBlqn8Qb

second times first ^yphiyAi0

The matrix that if you multiply a matrix by it remain unchanged, it has to 
be squared and has a oblique line of 1s ^LzQugc4u

The matrix, for which if you multiply the current matrix you are you get the identity matrix.
Because the identity matrix can be though of the number 1 when multiplying, the inverse is
the number that if you multiply by you get the number 1, the notation is A^-1.
It has to have the same rows as the columns of the other and the same columns as rows of
the other (90 flip) ^SzllHdad
